INSTRUCTIONS FOR THE TASK PLANNER ===\r\nReturn exclusively valid JSON.\r\nThe JSON object must contain a \"tasks\" array.\r\nEach task must contain: id, order, type, description, agent, suggested_action, depends_on, and parameters.\r\nDo not create any task to generate Word or DOCX files.\r\nFor text file generation only when explicitly requested, use suggested_action = \"CREATE_TEXT_DOCUMENT\".\r\nFor email delivery, use suggested_action = \"SEND_EMAIL\".\r\nIf an email must be sent and no explicit recipient is found, use [EMAIL]\r\nFor SEND_EMAIL, parameters.to must be [EMAIL] unless the original user prompt provides another recipient.\r\nFor browser navigation or interaction, use only allowed BROWSER_* actions.\r\nAllowed browser actions: BROWSER_NAVIGATE, BROWSER_SCREENSHOT.\r\nBefore BROWSER_SET_VALUE, BROWSER_CLICK, BROWSER_PRESS_ENTER, or BROWSER_SUBMIT_FORM, create a previous BROWSER_READ_PAGE or BROWSER_DOM_LIST task, unless an explicit CSS selector was provided.\r\nFor website searches: navigate, wait/map/read the page, fill the search field with BROWSER_SET_VALUE, submit using BROWSER_PRESS_ENTER with the same selector/index, then capture the results with BROWSER_CAPTURE_TEXT.\r\nDo not invent data that is not present in the user prompt, the DOM, or the captured real page content.\r\nIf the user asks to create a summary and send it by email, DO NOT generate CREATE_TEXT_DOCUMENT.\r\nThe summary for email must be generated by a cognitive/content task with suggested_action empty, then copied into the SEND_EMAIL body.\r\nDo not save TXT, DOCX, Word, or any local file when the user only asks to send the summary by email.\r\nFor a curriculum/resume captured from a website, first capture the text with BROWSER_CAPTURE_TEXT or BROWSER_READ_PAGE, then create a cognitive summary task, then send that generated summary in the email body.\r\nAccepted cognitive summary action names from the model, if it insists on one, are: CREATE_SUMMARY, CREATE_TEXT_SUMMARY, SUMMARIZE_TEXT, GENERATE_SUMMARY, ANALYZE_TEXT. Era Hygia quem atendia os casos antes do pai, realizando as atividades preventivas (ações ligadas a educação e higiene).\r\n\r\nPor favor identifique-se para prosseguir.\t\r\n\r\n=== MANDATORY INSTRUCTIONS FOR THE TASK PLANNER ===\r\nReturn exclusively valid JSON.\r\nThe JSON object must contain a \"tasks\" array.\r\nEach task must contain: id, order, type, description, agent, suggested_action, depends_on, and parameters.\r\nDo not create any task to generate Word or DOCX files.\r\nFor text file generation only when explicitly requested, use suggested_action = \"CREATE_TEXT_DOCUMENT\".\r\nFor email delivery, use suggested_action = \"SEND_EMAIL\".\r\nIf an email must be sent and no explicit recipient is found, use [EMAIL]\r\nFor SEND_EMAIL, parameters.to must be [EMAIL] unless the original user prompt provides another recipient.\r\nFor browser navigation or interaction, use only allowed BROWSER_* actions.\r\nAllowed browser actions: BROWSER_NAVIGATE, BROWSER_WAIT_SELECTOR, BROWSER_READ_PAGE, BROWSER_DOM_LIST, BROWSER_CAPTURE_TEXT, BROWSER_SET_VALUE, BROWSER_FOCUS, BROWSER_CLICK, BROWSER_PRESS_ENTER, BROWSER_SUBMIT_FORM, BROWSER_SCREENSHOT.\r\nBefore BROWSER_SET_VALUE, BROWSER_CLICK, BROWSER_PRESS_ENTER, or BROWSER_SUBMIT_FORM, create a previous BROWSER_READ_PAGE or BROWSER_DOM_LIST task, unless an explicit CSS selector was provided.\r\nFor website searches: navigate, wait/map/read the page, fill the search field with BROWSER_SET_VALUE, submit using BROWSER_PRESS_ENTER with the same selector/index, then capture the results with BROWSER_CAPTURE_TEXT.\r\nDo not invent data that is not present in the user prompt, the DOM, or the captured real page content.\r\nIf the user asks to create a summary and send it by email, DO NOT generate CREATE_TEXT_DOCUMENT.\r\nThe summary for email must be generated by a cognitive/content task with suggested_action empty, then copied into the SEND_EMAIL body.\r\nDo not save TXT, DOCX, Word, or any local file when the user only asks to send the summary by email.\r\nFor a curriculum/resume captured from a website, first capture the text with BROWSER_CAPTURE_TEXT or BROWSER_READ_PAGE, then create a cognitive summary task, then send that generated summary in the email body.\r\nAccepted cognitive summary action names from the model, if it insists on one, are: INSTRUCTIONS FOR THE TASK PLANNER ===\r\nReturn exclusively valid JSON.\r\nThe JSON object must contain a \"tasks\" array.\r\nEach task must contain: id, order, type, description, agent, suggested_action, depends_on, and parameters.\r\nDo not create any task to generate Word or DOCX files.\r\nFor text file generation only when explicitly requested, use suggested_action = \"CREATE_TEXT_DOCUMENT\".\r\nFor email delivery, use suggested_action = \"SEND_EMAIL\".\r\nIf an email must be sent and no explicit recipient is found, use [EMAIL]\r\nFor SEND_EMAIL, parameters.to must be [EMAIL] unless the original user prompt provides another recipient.\r\nFor browser navigation or interaction, use only allowed BROWSER_* actions.\r\nAllowed browser actions: BROWSER_NAVIGATE, BROWSER_WAIT_SELECTOR, BROWSER_READ_PAGE, BROWSER_DOM_LIST, BROWSER_CAPTURE_TEXT, BROWSER_SET_VALUE, BROWSER_FOCUS, BROWSER_CLICK, BROWSER_PRESS_ENTER, BROWSER_SUBMIT_FORM, BROWSER_SCREENSHOT.\r\nBefore BROWSER_SET_VALUE, BROWSER_CLICK, BROWSER_PRESS_ENTER, or BROWSER_SUBMIT_FORM, create a previous BROWSER_READ_PAGE or BROWSER_DOM_LIST task, unless an explicit CSS selector was provided.\r\nFor website searches: navigate, wait/map/read the page, fill the search field with BROWSER_SET_VALUE, submit using BROWSER_PRESS_ENTER with the same selector/index, then capture the results with BROWSER_CAPTURE_TEXT.\r\nDo not invent data that is not present in the user prompt, the DOM, or the captured real page content.\r\nIf the user asks to create a summary and send it by email, DO NOT generate CREATE_TEXT_DOCUMENT.\r\nThe summary for email must be generated by a cognitive/content task with suggested_action empty, then copied into the SEND_EMAIL body.\r\nDo not save TXT, DOCX, Word, or any local file when the user only asks to send the summary by email.\r\nFor a curriculum/resume captured from a website, first capture the text with BROWSER_CAPTURE_TEXT or BROWSER_READ_PAGE, then create a cognitive summary task, then send that generated summary in the email body.\r\nAccepted cognitive summary action names from the model, if it insists on one, are: CREATE_SUMMARY, CREATE_TEXT_SUMMARY, SUMMARIZE_TEXT, GENERATE_SUMMARY, ANALYZE_TEXT. The loader will convert them to an empty operational action.\r\nPreferred required format:\r\n{\r\n  \"tasks\": [\r\n    {\r\n      \"id\": \"T001\",\r\n      \"order\": 1,\r\n      \"type\": INSTRUCTIONS FOR THE TASK PLANNER ===\r\nReturn exclusively valid JSON.\r\nThe JSON object must contain a \"tasks\" array.\r\nEach task must contain: id, order, type, description, agent, suggested_action, depends_on, and parameters.\r\nDo not create any task to generate Word or DOCX files.\r\nFor text file generation only when explicitly requested, use suggested_action = \"CREATE_TEXT_DOCUMENT\".\r\nFor email delivery, use suggested_action = \"SEND_EMAIL\".\r\nIf an email must be sent and no explicit recipient is found, use [EMAIL]\r\nFor SEND_EMAIL, parameters.to must be [EMAIL] unless the original user prompt provides another recipient.\r\nFor browser navigation or interaction, use only allowed BROWSER_* actions.\r\nAllowed browser actions: BROWSER_NAVIGATE, BROWSER_WAIT_SELECTOR, BROWSER_READ_PAGE, BROWSER_DOM_LIST, BROWSER_CAPTURE_TEXT, BROWSER_SET_VALUE, BROWSER_FOCUS, BROWSER_CLICK, BROWSER_PRESS_ENTER, BROWSER_SUBMIT_FORM, BROWSER_SCREENSHOT.\r\nBefore BROWSER_SET_VALUE, BROWSER_CLICK, BROWSER_PRESS_ENTER, or BROWSER_SUBMIT_FORM, create a previous BROWSER_READ_PAGE or BROWSER_DOM_LIST task, unless an explicit CSS selector was provided.\r\nFor website searches: navigate, wait/map/read the page, fill the search field with BROWSER_SET_VALUE, submit using BROWSER_PRESS_ENTER with the same selector/index, then capture the results with BROWSER_CAPTURE_TEXT.\r\nDo not invent data that is not present in the user prompt, the DOM, or the captured real page content.\r\nIf the user asks to create a summary and send it by email, DO NOT generate CREATE_TEXT_DOCUMENT.\r\nThe summary for email must be generated by a cognitive/content task with suggested_action empty, then copied into the SEND_EMAIL body.\r\nDo not save TXT, DOCX, Word, or any local file when the user only asks to send the summary by email.\r\nFor a curriculum/resume captured from a website, first capture the text with BROWSER_CAPTURE_TEXT or BROWSER_READ_PAGE, then create a cognitive summary task, then send that generated summary in the email body.\r\nAccepted cognitive summary action names from the model, if it insists on one, are: CREATE_SUMMARY, CREATE_TEXT_SUMMARY, SUMMARIZE_TEXT, GENERATE_SUMMARY, ANALYZE_TEXT. The loader will convert them to an empty operational action.\r\nPreferred required format:\r\n{\r\n  \"tasks\": [\r\n    {\r\n      \"id\": \"T001\",\r\n      \"order\": 1,\r\n      \"type\":
